Scene,General/EditorPointLight,122013,121963,1,0,0,0,PointLight,343.45,1068.565,-126.8058,0,0,0,4,4,4,None,Entities,Default,DefaultNoTint|255/255/255/255,PointLight|Color:255/0/0/255|Intensity:1|Range:100
/// Logic
class Main
{   
    Description = "Survive multiple waves of spooky titans.";
    StartTitans = 3;
    AddTitansPerWave = 1;
    MaxWaves = 20;
    RespawnOnWave = true;
    GradualSpawn = true;
    GradualSpawnTooltip = "Spawn new titans gradually over time. Helpful for reducing lag.";
    PumpkinHookable = true;
    _currentWave = 0;
    _hasSpawned = false;
    _jumpscare = false;

    function OnGameStart()
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient)
        {
            self.NextWave();
        }
    }

    function OnCharacterSpawn(character)
    {
        if (character.Type == "Titan")
        {

            if (character.IsMine)
            {
                if (character.DetectRange > 0)
                {
                    character.DetectRange = 2000;
                }
            }

            head = character.HeadMount;
            ps = head.Position;
            size = character.Size;

            x = ps.X;
            y = ps.Y + 8 * (size / 3);
            z = ps.Z;

            rx = 0;
            ry = 90;
            rz = 0;

            sx = size * 4;
            sy = size * 4;
            sz = size * 4;

            # Spawn a pumpkin on the titan's head
            pos =   "" + x  + "," + y  + "," + z ;
            rot =   "" + rx + "," + ry + "," + rz;
            scale = "" + sx + "," + sy + "," + sz;
            trs = pos + "," + rot + "," + scale;
            # a,b,c,d options for pumpkin head
            selection = Random.RandomInt(0, 4);
            name = "Decor/Pumpkin1";
            if (selection == 0)
            {
                name += "a";
            }
            elif (selection == 1)
            {
                name += "b";
            }
            elif (selection == 2)
            {
                name += "c";
            }
            else
            {
                name += "d";
            }
            collisionMode = "None,Projectiles";
            if (self.PumpkinHookable)
            {
                collisionMode = "Physical,Projectiles";
            }
            jack = Map.CreateMapObjectRaw("Scene,"+name+",0,0,1,0,1,0,PumpkinHead,"+trs+","+collisionMode+",Default,Default|255/255/255/255");
            jack.Parent = head;
            jack.Forward = head.Forward;

            # Rotate jack 90 degrees to the right
            jack.LocalRotation = Vector3(0, 90, 0);

        }
    }

    function SpawnObject(object, name, ps, rt, sz)
    {
        # Spawn a pumpkin on the titan's head
        pos =   "" + ps.X  + "," + ps.Y  + "," + ps.Z;
        rot =   "" + rt.X + "," + rt.Y + "," + rt.Z;
        scale = "" + sz.X + "," + sz.Y + "," + sz.Z;
        trs = pos + "," + rot + "," + scale;
        Game.Print("Spawning object: " + object + " at " + trs);
        return Map.CreateMapObjectRaw("Scene,"+object+",0,0,1,0,1,0,"+name+","+trs+",Physical,Projectiles,Default,Default|255/255/255/255");
    }


    coroutine Jumpscare()
    {
        if (Network.MyPlayer.Character == null)
        {
            return;
        }
        self._jumpscare = true;
        type = "Decor/Darwin1";
        name = "Jumpscare";
        ps = Vector3(120, 0, 0);
        ps = Network.MyPlayer.Character.Position + ps;
        rt = Vector3(0, 0, 0);
        sz = Vector3(1, 1, 1);
        object = self.SpawnObject(type, name, ps, rt, sz);

        # Wait for 1 second
        wait 3.0;

        # Destroy the jumpscare
        Map.DestroyMapObject(object, false);
        self._jumpscare = false;
    }

    function OnTick()
    {
        # Jumpscare :^)
        # if (Random.RandomInt(0, 100) < 10 && self._jumpscare == false)
        # {
        #     self.Jumpscare();
        # }

        if (Network.IsMasterClient && !Game.IsEnding)
        {
            titans = Game.Titans.Count;
            humans = Game.Humans.Count;
		    playerShifters = Game.PlayerShifters.Count;
            if (humans > 0 || playerShifters > 0)
            {
                self._hasSpawned = true;
            }
            if (titans == 0)
            {
                self.NextWave();
            }
            if (humans == 0 && playerShifters == 0 && self._hasSpawned)
            {
                UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Humanity failed!");
                Game.End(10.0);
                return;
            }
            UI.SetLabelAll("TopCenter", "Titans Left: " + Convert.ToString(titans) + "  " + "Wave: " + Convert.ToString(self._currentWave));
        }
    }

    function NextWave()
    {
        self._currentWave = self._currentWave + 1;
        if (self._currentWave > self.MaxWaves)
        {
            UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "All waves cleared, humanity wins!");
            Game.End(10.0);
            return;
        }
        amount = self.AddTitansPerWave * (self._currentWave - 1) + self.StartTitans;
        if (self.GradualSpawn)
        {
            Game.SpawnTitansAsync("Default", amount);
        }
        else
        {
            Game.SpawnTitans("Default", amount);
        }
        if (self.RespawnOnWave)
        {
            Game.SpawnPlayerAll(false);
        }
    }
}

component EyeTracker {
    TrackTimer = 10;
    Limit = 40;

    _startRotation = null;
    _timer = 0;
    _trackedPlayer = null;

    function Init()
    {
        self._startRotation = self.MapObject.Rotation;
        self._trackedPlayer = self.FindClosestPlayer();
    }

    function OnTick()
    {
        if (self._timer > 0)
        {
            self._timer = self._timer - Time.TickTime;
        }
        else
        {
            self._timer = self.TrackTimer;
            self._trackedPlayer = self.FindClosestPlayer();
        }
        if (self._trackedPlayer != null)
        {
            # Look at opposite of player
            target = self.SubtractVector3(self._trackedPlayer.Position, self.MapObject.Position);
            target = self.SubtractVector3(self.MapObject.Position, target);
            self.MapObject.Transform.LookAt(target);
        }
    }

    function SubtractVector3(a, b)
    {
        return Vector3(a.X - b.X, a.Y - b.Y, a.Z - b.Z);
    }

    function FindClosestPlayer()
    {
        closestPlayer = null;
        closestDistance = 9999999;
        for (player in Game.Humans)
        {
            if (player != null)
            {
                distance = Vector3.Distance(self.MapObject.Position, player.Position);
                if (distance < closestDistance)
                {
                    closestDistance = distance;
                    closestPlayer = player;
                }
            }
        }
        return closestPlayer;
    }
}
